## RESIDENT INDIVUALS INCOME TAX RATES WITH EFFECT FROM 1ST JULY, 2023

| Monthly Income                                                                       | Tax Rate                                                                    |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Where the total income does not exceed Tshs. 270,000/=                               | NIL                                                                         |
| Where the total income exceeds Tshs. 270,000/= but does not exceed Tshs. 520,000/=   | 8% of the amount in excess of Tshs. 270,000/=                               |
| Where the total income exceeds Tshs. 520,000/= but does not exceed Tshs. 760,000/=   | Tshs. 20,000/= plus 20% of the amount in excess of Tshs. 520,000/=          |
| Where the total income exceeds Tshs. 760,000/= but does not exceed Tshs. 1,000,000/= | Tshs. 68,000/= plus 25% of the amount in excess of Tshs. 760,000/=          |
| Where the total income exceeds Tshs. 1,000,000/=                                     | Tshs. 128,000/= plus 30% of the amount in excess of Tshs. 1,000,000/=       |
| Note: Threshold per annum: Annual Income of Tshs 3,240,000/= is not taxable          | Note: Threshold per annum: Annual Income of Tshs 3,240,000/= is not taxable |

## Worked example:

Income of Tshs. 520,000/= Tax is (520,000-270,000) x 8%=Tshs. 20,000/= Income of Tshs. 760,000/= Tax is 20,000 + (760,000-520,000) x 20%=Tshs. 68,000/= Income of Tshs. 1,000,000/= Tax is 68,000 + (1,000,000-760,000) x 25%=Tshs. 128,000/= Income of Tshs. 1,240,000/= Tax is 128,000 + (1,240,000-1,000,000) x 30%=Tshs.

200,000/=

T

## shs

## Note:

- i. For non-resident employees of a resident employer, the income, subject to withholding tax is the total income of a non-resident individual and is charged at a rate of 30%.
- ii. For an employee who makes a donation as per section 12 of Education Fund  Act 2001, such donation is exempted from tax. However exemption is granted upon approval by the Commissioner.

## Benefit  in  kind.

- a. Housing: Payment consisting of provision of premises by employer for residential by the employee:-

Is the market value of rental of premises or (i) or (ii) below, whichever is the lesser

- i. 15% of the employees total annual income and ;
- ii. The expenditure claimed as deduction by the employer in respect of the premises during the year of income.
- b. Car:  Motor  vehicle  taxable  benefits  are  based  of  the  engine  size and

vehicle age on the following annual values:

| Engine size           | Vehicle age up to 5 years Tshs.   | Greater than 5 years old Tshs.   |
|-----------------------|-----------------------------------|----------------------------------|
| Not exceeding 1000 cc | 250,000/-                         | 125,000/-                        |
| 1000 - 2000 cc        | 500,000/-                         | 250,000/-                        |
| 2000 - 3000 cc        | 1,000,000/-                       | 500,000/-                        |
| Above 3000 cc         | 1,500,000/-                       | 750,000/-                        |

Note: Benefit is not chargeable where the employer does not claim deduction in respect of the ownership, maintenance, or operation of the vehicle.

- c. Other Benefits : Market value will apply for quantification of other benefits in kind.

## PAYE &amp; SDL RETURNS AND PAYMENT

##  Payment of monthly PAYE &amp; SDL

Payment of PAYE and SDL should be within seven days after the month of glyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt; salary deduction.

##  Monthly SDL and PAYE return

An employer is obliged to submit the SDL and PAYE monthly return to TRA glyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt; showing  number  of  employees  and  levy  paid  within  seven  days  after  the glyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt; month of salary deduction.

##  Skills Development Levy (SDL)

Rate is glyph&lt;c=22,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;glyph&lt;c=17,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;glyph&lt;c=24,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt; % of the monthly gross emolument for Tanzania Mainland.

##  Monthly PAYE return

An employer is obliged to submit the PAYE return to TRA  showing employment taxes withheld respectively within seven days after the month of salary pay. glyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;

## Exempted employers from SDL

- Dglyph&lt;c=12,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt; $glyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt; *RYHUQPHQWglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;'HSDUWPHQWglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;RUglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;Dglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;3XEOLFglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;,QVWLWXWLRQglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;ZKLFKglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;LVglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;ZKROO\glyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt; LQDQFHGglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;E\glyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt;WKHglyph&lt;c=3,font=/OJWQWF+ArialMT&gt; Government

## Note

The gross emoluments include wages, salary, leave pay, sick pay, payment in lieu of leave, fees, commission, gratuity, bonuses, any subsistence, travelling or entertainment allowances.
